        <script>
        function loadRecipeOverlay1(button) {
            // التحقق من أن المحتوى لم يُحمل من قبل
            if (document.getElementById('recipeOverlay1')) {
                document.getElementById('recipeOverlay1').classList.add('active');
                document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
                var searchInput = document.getElementById('recipeSearchInput1');
                if (searchInput) {
                    searchInput.focus();
                }
                return;
            }
            
            // إنشاء عنصر التحميل
            var loadingDiv = document.createElement('div');
            loadingDiv.innerHTML = `
                <div style="position: fixed; top: 0; left: 0; width: 100%; height: 100%; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.8); z-index: 10000; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;">
                    <div style="background: white; padding: 30px; border-radius: 8px; text-align: center;">
                        <div style="width: 40px; height: 40px; border: 4px solid #f3f3f3; border-top: 4px solid #007cba; border-radius: 50%; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 0 auto 15px;"></div>
                        <p style="margin: 0; color: #666;">Loading Recipe Search...</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <style>@keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }</style>
            `;
            document.body.appendChild(loadingDiv);
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            
            // تأخير بسيط لإظهار التحميل ثم تحميل المحتوى
            setTimeout(function() {
                loadingDiv.remove();
                insertRecipeContent1();
            }, 300);
        }

                    <div class="recipe-slide-img"><picture><source srcset="https://www.alvarecipes.com/wp-content/webp-express/webp-images/uploads/2025/06/Recipes-Using-Frozen-Strawberries-The-Best-Ways-for-Year-Round-Deliciousness-150x150.jpg.webp" type="image/webp"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.alvarecipes.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/Recipes-Using-Frozen-Strawberries-The-Best-Ways-for-Year-Round-Deliciousness-150x150.jpg" alt="Recipes Using Frozen Strawberries The Best Ways for Year-Round Deliciousness" loading="lazy" class="webpexpress-processed"></picture></div>

                <a href="https://www.alvarecipes.com/ninja-creami-recipes-9-frozen-treats/">
                    <div class="recipe-slide-img"><picture><source srcset="https://www.alvarecipes.com/wp-content/webp-express/webp-images/uploads/2025/06/Cookie-Dough-Mix-In-Ice-Cream-150x150.jpg.webp" type="image/webp"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.alvarecipes.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/Cookie-Dough-Mix-In-Ice-Cream-150x150.jpg" alt="Best Ninja Creami Recipes You Must Try" loading="lazy" class="webpexpress-processed"></picture></div>
                    <div class="recipe-slide-content">
                        <span class="recipe-slide-category">Desserts</span>
                        <h4>Best Ninja Creami Recipes You Must&hellip;</h4>
                        <span class="recipe-slide-date">Juni 24, 2025</span>
                    </div>
                </a>
            </div>
            <div class="recipe-slide">
                <a href="https://www.alvarecipes.com/ninja-creami-recipes-9-must-try-flavors/">
                    <div class="recipe-slide-img"><picture><source srcset="https://www.alvarecipes.com/wp-content/webp-express/webp-images/uploads/2025/06/Ninja-Creami-Recipes-150x150.jpg.webp" type="image/webp"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.alvarecipes.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/Ninja-Creami-Recipes-150x150.jpg" alt="Ninja Creami Recipes" loading="lazy" class="webpexpress-processed"></picture></div>
                    <div class="recipe-slide-content">
                        <span class="recipe-slide-category">Desserts</span>
                        <h4>Ninja Creami Recipes: 9 Irresistible Flavors&hellip;</h4>
                        <span class="recipe-slide-date">Juni 20, 2025</span>
                    </div>
                </a>
            </div>                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                                            </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            `;
            
            // إدراج HTML في الصفحة
            document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', overlayHTML);
            
            // تهيئة الوظائف
            initRecipeOverlayFunctions1();
            
            // إظهار الـ overlay
            document.getElementById('recipeOverlay1').classList.add('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            var searchInput = document.getElementById('recipeSearchInput1');
            if (searchInput) {
                searchInput.focus();
            }
        }
        
        function closeRecipeOverlay1() {
            var overlay = document.getElementById('recipeOverlay1');
            if (overlay) {
                overlay.classList.remove('active');
            }
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }
        
        function initRecipeOverlayFunctions1() {
            var overlay = document.getElementById('recipeOverlay1');
            var searchInput = document.getElementById('recipeSearchInput1');
            var searchBtn = document.getElementById('recipeSearchBtn1');
            var categoryFilter = document.getElementById('recipeCategoryFilter1');
            var searchResults = document.getElementById('recipeSearchResults1');
            var searchGrid = document.getElementById('recipeSearchGrid1');
            var searchTitle = document.getElementById('recipeSearchTitle1');
            var searchCount = document.getElementById('recipeSearchCount1');
            var loadMoreSection = document.getElementById('recipeSearchLoadMore1');
            var loadMoreBtn = document.getElementById('recipeLoadMoreBtn1');
            
            if (!overlay || !searchInput || !searchBtn || !categoryFilter || !searchResults || !searchGrid || !searchTitle || !searchCount || !loadMoreSection || !loadMoreBtn) {
                return;
            }
            
            var ajaxUrl = 'https://www.alvarecipes.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php';
            var searchNonce = '440c633ad4';
            var sliderNonce = '954fd67754';

            var currentSearchPage = 1;
            var currentSearchTerm = '';
            var currentCategory = 'all';
            var hasMoreSearchResults = false;

            // إغلاق الـ Overlay
            overlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (e.target === overlay) {
                    closeRecipeOverlay1();
                }
            });

            // إغلاق بالـ Escape
            document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
                if (e.key === 'Escape' && overlay && overlay.classList.contains('active')) {
                    closeRecipeOverlay1();
                }
            });

            // ===== وظائف البحث =====
            var searchTimeout;
            var isSearching = false;

            function performSearch(page, append) {
                if (isSearching) return;
                
                page = page || 1;
                append = append || false;
                
                var searchTerm = searchInput.value.trim();
                var category = categoryFilter.value;

                if (!append) {
                    currentSearchPage = 1;
                    currentSearchTerm = searchTerm;
                    currentCategory = category;
                }

                if (searchTerm.length < 2 && category === 'all') {
                    searchResults.style.display = 'none';
                    return;
                }

                isSearching = true;
                searchResults.style.display = 'block';
                var loadingEl = searchResults.querySelector('.recipe-search-loading');
                if (loadingEl) {
                    loadingEl.style.display = 'block';
                }
                loadMoreSection.style.display = 'none';
                
                if (!append) {
                    searchGrid.innerHTML = '';
                }

                var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
                xhr.open('POST', ajaxUrl);
                xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
                
                xhr.onreadystatechange = function() {
                    if (xhr.readyState === 4) {
                        isSearching = false;
                        if (loadingEl) {
                            loadingEl.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                        
                        if (xhr.status === 200) {
                            try {
                                var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
                                if (response.success && response.data && response.data.html) {
                                    if (append) {
                                        searchGrid.innerHTML += response.data.html;
                                    } else {
                                        searchGrid.innerHTML = response.data.html;
                                    }
                                    
                                    var resultText = searchTerm ? 'Search Results' : 'Category: ' + getCategoryName(category);
                                    searchTitle.textContent = resultText;
                                    searchCount.textContent = (response.data.total_found || 0) + ' recipes found';
                                    
                                    hasMoreSearchResults = response.data.has_more || false;
                                    currentSearchPage = response.data.current_page || 1;
                                    
                                    if (hasMoreSearchResults) {
                                        loadMoreSection.style.display = 'block';
                                        loadMoreBtn.disabled = false;
                                        loadMoreBtn.textContent = 'Load More Results';
                                    } else {
                                        loadMoreSection.style.display = 'none';
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    if (!append) {
                                        searchGrid.innerHTML = '<div class="recipe-no-results">No recipes found. Try different keywords or category.</div>';
                                        searchCount.textContent = '0 recipes found';
                                        loadMoreSection.style.display = 'none';
                                    }
                                }
                            } catch(e) {
                                if (!append) {
                                    searchGrid.innerHTML = '<div class="recipe-error">Search error. Please try again.</div>';
                                }
                            }
                        } else {
                            if (!append) {
                                searchGrid.innerHTML = '<div class="recipe-error">Search error. Please try again.</div>';
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };

                var params = 'action=recipe_search&nonce=' + encodeURIComponent(searchNonce) + '&search=' + encodeURIComponent(searchTerm) + '&category=' + encodeURIComponent(category) + '&page=' + encodeURIComponent(page);
                xhr.send(params);
            }

            function getCategoryName(slug) {
                if (slug === 'all') return 'All Categories';
                var option = categoryFilter.querySelector('[value="' + slug + '"]');
                return option ? option.textContent : slug;
            }

            // البحث عند الكتابة
            searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
                searchTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
                    performSearch(1, false);
                }, 500);
            });

            // البحث عند النقر
            searchBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                performSearch(1, false);
            });

            // البحث عند تغيير التصنيف
            categoryFilter.addEventListener('change', function() {
                performSearch(1, false);
            });

            // البحث عند الضغط على Enter
            searchInput.addEventListener('keypress', function(e) {
                if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    performSearch(1, false);
                }
            });

            // Load More للبحث
            loadMoreBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                if (hasMoreSearchResults && !isSearching) {
                    loadMoreBtn.disabled = true;
                    loadMoreBtn.textContent = 'Loading...';
                    performSearch(currentSearchPage + 1, true);
                }
            });

            // ===== وظائف السلايدر =====
            var sliders = overlay.querySelectorAll('.recipe-slider');

            sliders.forEach(function(slider) {
                var isLoading = false;
                var currentPage = 0;
                var hasMore = true;
                var allSlides = [];
                var currentOffset = parseInt(slider.dataset.currentOffset) || 0;
                
                var initialSlides = Array.from(slider.querySelectorAll('.recipe-slide'));
                allSlides = initialSlides.slice();

                var loadingIndicator = overlay.querySelector('#recipe-loading-' + slider.dataset.slider);
                
                function getVisibleCount() {
                    if (window.innerWidth >= 1200) return 5;
                    if (window.innerWidth >= 900) return 4;
                    if (window.innerWidth >= 600) return 3;
                    return 2;
                }

                function showPage(pageNum) {
                    var visibleCount = getVisibleCount();
                    var startIndex = pageNum * visibleCount;
                    var endIndex = startIndex + visibleCount;
                    
                    allSlides.forEach(function(slide) {
                        slide.style.display = 'none';
                    });
                    
                    var pageSlides = allSlides.slice(startIndex, endIndex);
                    pageSlides.forEach(function(slide) {
                        slide.style.display = 'block';
                    });
                    
                    slider.style.transform = 'translateX(0)';
                    currentPage = pageNum;
                    updateButtons();
                }

                function updateButtons() {
                    var prevBtn = overlay.querySelector('[data-target="' + slider.dataset.slider + '"].recipe-prev');
                    var nextBtn = overlay.querySelector('[data-target="' + slider.dataset.slider + '"].recipe-next');
                    var visibleCount = getVisibleCount();
                    var maxPage = Math.ceil(allSlides.length / visibleCount) - 1;
                    
                    if (prevBtn) prevBtn.disabled = currentPage === 0;
                    if (nextBtn) nextBtn.disabled = currentPage >= maxPage && !hasMore;
                }

                function showLoading() {
                    if (loadingIndicator) loadingIndicator.classList.add('active');
                }

                function hideLoading() {
                    if (loadingIndicator) loadingIndicator.classList.remove('active');
                }

                function loadMoreSlides(targetPage, callback) {
                    if (isLoading || !hasMore) return callback(false);
                    
                    var visibleCount = getVisibleCount();
                    var requiredSlides = (targetPage + 1) * visibleCount;
                    
                    if (allSlides.length >= requiredSlides) return callback(true);
                    
                    isLoading = true;
                    showLoading();

                    var slidesToLoad = Math.max(visibleCount * 2, requiredSlides - allSlides.length);
                    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
                    xhr.open('POST', ajaxUrl);
                    xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
                    
                    xhr.onreadystatechange = function() {
                        if (xhr.readyState === 4) {
                            isLoading = false;
                            hideLoading();
                            
                            if (xhr.status === 200) {
                                try {
                                    var response = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
                                    if (response.success && response.data && response.data.html) {
                                        var tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
                                        tempDiv.innerHTML = response.data.html;
                                        
                                        var newSlides = Array.from(tempDiv.querySelectorAll('.recipe-slide'));
                                        if (newSlides.length > 0) {
                                            newSlides.forEach(function(slide) {
                                                slide.style.display = 'none';
                                                slider.appendChild(slide);
                                                allSlides.push(slide);
                                            });
                                            
                                            currentOffset = response.data.offset || (currentOffset + newSlides.length);
                                            hasMore = response.data.has_more || false;
                                            callback(true);
                                        } else {
                                            hasMore = false;
                                            callback(false);
                                        }
                                    } else {
                                        hasMore = false;
                                        callback(false);
                                    }
                                } catch(e) {
                                    hasMore = false;
                                    callback(false);
                                }
                            } else {
                                hasMore = false;
                                callback(false);
                            }
                        }
                    };

                    var params = 'action=recipe_load_more&nonce=' + encodeURIComponent(sliderNonce) + '&section_type=' + encodeURIComponent(slider.dataset.section) + '&offset=' + encodeURIComponent(currentOffset) + '&posts_per_page=' + encodeURIComponent(slidesToLoad);
                    xhr.send(params);
                }

                function goToPage(targetPage) {
                    var visibleCount = getVisibleCount();
                    var maxCurrentPage = Math.ceil(allSlides.length / visibleCount) - 1;
                    
                    if (targetPage > maxCurrentPage) {
                        loadMoreSlides(targetPage, function(success) {
                            if (success) showPage(targetPage);
                        });
                    } else {
                        showPage(targetPage);
                    }
                }

                // معالج النقر على الأزرار
                overlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    if (e.target.dataset.target === slider.dataset.slider) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        
                        if (e.target.classList.contains('recipe-prev') && currentPage > 0) {
                            showPage(currentPage - 1);
                        } else if (e.target.classList.contains('recipe-next')) {
                            goToPage(currentPage + 1);
                        }
                    }
                });

                // دعم اللمس للهواتف
                var touchStartX = 0;
                var touchStartY = 0;
                var isSwiping = false;

                slider.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) {
                    touchStartX = e.touches[0].clientX;
                    touchStartY = e.touches[0].clientY;
                    isSwiping = false;
                });

                slider.addEventListener('touchmove', function(e) {
                    if (!touchStartX || !touchStartY) return;
                    
                    var touchCurrentX = e.touches[0].clientX;
                    var touchCurrentY = e.touches[0].clientY;
                    var diffX = touchStartX - touchCurrentX;
                    var diffY = touchStartY - touchCurrentY;
                    
                    if (Math.abs(diffX) > Math.abs(diffY) && Math.abs(diffX) > 10) {
                        isSwiping = true;
                        e.preventDefault();
                    }
                });

                slider.addEventListener('touchend', function(e) {
                    if (!isSwiping || !touchStartX) return;
                    
                    var touchEndX = e.changedTouches[0].clientX;
                    var diff = touchStartX - touchEndX;
                    
                    if (Math.abs(diff) > 50) {
                        if (diff > 0) {
                            goToPage(currentPage + 1);
                        } else if (currentPage > 0) {
                            showPage(currentPage - 1);
                        }
                    }
                    
                    touchStartX = 0;
                    touchStartY = 0;
                    isSwiping = false;
                });

                // عرض الصفحة الأولى
                showPage(0);
                
                // إعادة تعيين عند تغيير حجم الشاشة
                var resizeTimeout;
                window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
                    clearTimeout(resizeTimeout);
                    resizeTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
                        var visibleCount = getVisibleCount();
                        var newMaxPage = Math.ceil(allSlides.length / visibleCount) - 1;
                        currentPage = Math.min(currentPage, newMaxPage);
                        showPage(currentPage);
                    }, 150);
                });
            });
        }
        </script>
        
</div>
</div>

<div>
<div class="gb-element-705ced21">
